- Do not implement Arachne vibration in WORLD or via per-vertex deformation. WORLD is intentionally still per §8.2 anchor-vs-tip physics — silk shakes against a stationary forest. Arachne is a fullscreen-fragment preset; per-vertex deformation would require a vertex stage which Arachne does not have. Vibration is a fragment-space UV jitter on COMPOSITE web walks (`arachneEvalWeb(vibUV, ...)`) + spider body translation only. The bottom-of-fragment `worldTex.sample(...)` keeps the original `uv`. D-094.
- Do not advance Arachne build stages in beats. Build pace is audio-modulated TIME (`dt × pace`, where `pace = 1.0 + 0.18 × midAttRel + max(0, 0.5 × drumsEnergyDev)`). V.7.5's beat-measured stage timing was admitted in `ARACHNE_V8_DESIGN.md §5.2` to be wrong (inconsistent build cadence across tracks). The pause guard MUST be evaluated BEFORE `effectiveDt` is computed — if you compute `dt × pace` first and then zero it on spider activity, the spider blend ramp time bleeds into the build timeline. D-095.
- Do not add the V.7.5 4-web pool back as the foreground rendering source. The post-V.7.7C.2 composition is ONE foreground hero web (driven by `webs[0]` Row 5 BuildState) + 1–2 saturated background webs at depth (V.7.5 spawn/eviction continues to run for `webs[1..3]` as background depth context only). Spawn / eviction logic was retired for the FOREGROUND; if you find yourself making the foreground anchor block read `webs[0].stage` / `webs[0].progress` (Row 2) instead of Row 5 fields, stop — that's V.7.5 thinking. The shader's pool loop starts at `wi = 1` for the same reason. D-095.
- Do not call `arachneState.reset()` outside `applyPreset`'s `.staged` branch. The build state machine's segment start is the canonical reset point; ad-hoc resets break per-segment spider cooldown semantics (`spiderFiredInSegment` would clear at the wrong time, allowing the spider to re-trigger mid-segment). The visual-review harness (`PresetVisualReviewTests`) deliberately skips `reset()` because it doesn't simulate orchestrator segment boundaries — that's why the harness renders the foreground in frame phase at low progress. D-095.
- Do not gate the chord spiral on per-ring visibility. Per-ring `kVis = (k / N_RINGS) <= progress` makes an entire ring's chord segments + drops appear at once as a complete oval — Matt's 2026-05-08T17-01-15Z manual smoke flagged this as the §5.6 "spider lays chords one-at-a-time" violation. Use the V.7.7C.3 per-chord gate `globalChordIdx < int(progress × N_RINGS × nSpk)` so chords reveal outside-in by ring, clockwise-by-spoke within. D-095.
- Do not re-enable the V.7.5 pool web rendering loop. Matt's 2026-05-08 manual smoke flagged the V.7.5 spawn/eviction churn ("full webs flash on and fade away ... new webs form over the central web being spun") as competing with the foreground build, not framing it. V.7.7C.3 changed the shader's pool loop bound from `wi < kArachWebs` to `wi < 1` (empty body) and the foreground hero is now the only rendered web for Arachne. CPU-side V.7.5 spawn state still advances harmlessly so unit tests pass; if you find yourself raising the bound back to `kArachWebs`, stop. The §5.12 1–2 saturated background webs need a separate slot-8 buffer flush for `ArachneBackgroundWeb`, NOT a re-enabled V.7.5 pool. D-095.
- Do not gate the spider trigger on `subBass + bassAttackRatio < 0.55`. Live LTYL session data (2026-05-08T17-01-15Z) confirmed this combination is acoustically impossible on real music: kicks have `subBass > 0.30` but `bassAttackRatio > 1.0` (sharp transient against AGC); sustained sub-bass passages have `subBass` near AGC average. The 0.75 s sustain accumulator decays at 2× rate during sub-threshold frames so it never reaches threshold on either pattern. V.7.7C.3 trigger is `features.bassAttRel > 0.30` (smoothed bass envelope — same primitive the §8.2 vibration uses successfully); brief kick pulses are filtered by the existing 0.75 s sustain accumulator unaided. Failed Approach #57. D-095.
- Do not pack per-segment Arachne polygon state into `webs[0]` Row 5 or a new WebGPU row. Row 5 fields (`build_stage` / `frame_progress` / `radial_packed` / `spiral_packed`) are the V.7.7C.2 BuildState contract; adding more fields would push the struct stride past 96 bytes. V.7.7C.3 packs the polygon anchor indices into the existing `webs[0].rngSeed` field (UInt32, byte offset 28) via `ArachneState.packPolygonAnchors(_:)` — the V.7.5 spawn driver no longer consumes that field on the shader side after Fix 2 retired pool rendering. If you need additional per-foreground state beyond what fits in `rngSeed` (32 bits) and Row 5, allocate a side buffer at slot 8 instead. D-095.
- Do not parameterize `ProceduralGeometry` to host a non-Murmuration particle preset's behavior. Particle presets are siblings, not subclasses (D-097). The `["feedback", "particles"]` pass is dispatched through the `ParticleGeometry` protocol (`update`, `render`, `activeParticleFraction`); each preset ships its own conformer rather than parameterizing `ProceduralGeometry`'s kernel-name lookup, particle count, drag, or `decayRate: 0` flock-persistence semantics. Drift Motes (DM.1) ships `DriftMotesGeometry` with its own `motes_update` kernel and sprite vertex/fragment functions; future particle presets do the same. If you find yourself adding a new field to `ParticleConfiguration` because Murmuration doesn't use it, stop — that field belongs in a new conformer's private state.
- Do not extend an MSL struct in `Common.metal` (or any engine library shared file) without verifying byte-identical reads via `PresetRegressionTests` golden-hash regen across every preset. The DM.2 `FeatureVector` 32 → 48-float and `StemFeatures` 16 → 64-float extension (D-099) was safe because the first 32 / 16 floats kept their original offsets — Murmuration's `particle_update`, MVWarp's vertex/fragment, and `feedback_warp_fragment` all read fields in the original tail. If a future struct edit reorders existing fields or inserts a new field anywhere in the original tail, every engine-library reader's byte access shifts and silent visual regressions land. The Swift-side `CommonLayoutTest` regression-locks the sizes against shrinkage; the golden-hash sweep is the load-bearing visual check. D-099.

- **Increment BUG-011 ⏳ 2026-05-10 — Arachne over Tier 2 frame budget: tuning levers L1+L2+L3 + SOAK kernel-cost benchmark.** Four-commit perf increment (`082164c7..bd213856`); status remains **Open** in [docs/QUALITY/KNOWN_ISSUES.md](docs/QUALITY/KNOWN_ISSUES.md) because closure requires Matt's M2 Pro real-music perf capture per [docs/diagnostics/DM.3-perf-capture.md](docs/diagnostics/DM.3-perf-capture.md). Pre-tuning baseline (session `2026-05-08T22-01-07Z`, 4,579 Arachne frames on M2 Pro): p50 = 14.120 ms, p95 = 26.607 ms, p99 = 32.743 ms — 53 % over the 14 ms FrameBudgetManager downshift threshold at the median. **Three shader-side levers pulled, each in its own commit with golden-hash + visual + test verification at every step.** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/Arachne.metal](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/Arachne.metal): **L1 (`082164c7`)** spider ray-march `maxSteps = 32 → 24` (the 0.15 UV spider patch ~226×226 px @ 1080p ran the full 32-step worst case for every miss-ray; on-hit rays unaffected — sphere trace early-exits at hitEps); **L2 (`1643ee24`)** drop refraction coverage gate `wr.dropCov > 0.01 → > 0.5` at both anchor + dead-pool sites (the 0.01 floor admitted the entire anti-aliased rim band of every drop into the `worldTex.sample(refractedUV)` path; drops now render with a clean visible core, rim pixels fall through to the silk-strand colour underneath); **L3 (`96b2c288`)** spider dispatch gate `spider.blend > 0.01 → > 0.05` at the dispatch site only, NOT the overlay mix (`listenLiftEMA` is not plumbed to the GPU per D-094, so the gate uses `spider.blend` alone — listening pose triggers via the existing path with at most a 1-frame lag). **SOAK kernel-cost benchmark (`bd213856`):** [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Diagnostics/SoakTestHarnessTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Diagnostics/SoakTestHarnessTests.swift) — new `shortRunArachneComposite` test mirrors the existing `shortRunDriftMotes` pattern but renders Arachne's COMPOSITE fragment to a 1920×1080 offscreen texture with the spider forced active (worst case — patch ray-march fires every frame). SOAK_TESTS=1 gated; `@testable import Presets` added to imports. **M2 Pro post-L1+L2+L3 measurement (this session):** kernel p50 = 12.724 ms / p95 = 14.458 ms / p99 = 15.169 ms / mean = 12.903 ms across 1800 frames; 172 of 1800 frames (~10 %) over 14 ms; run-to-run variance ≈ 0.1 ms. **Calibration finding worth preserving:** the Drift Motes kernel:full-pipeline ratio of ~1:3 does NOT apply to Arachne — Arachne is fragment-only (no compute pre-pass to add on top), so kernel ≈ full-pipeline. The initial 5 ms SOAK gate suggested by the BUG-011 prompt was anchored on the wrong ratio and was rebased to **16 ms p95** based on the in-session measurement (~10 % above the worst-case fixture, well below the pre-tuning ~26 ms baseline a lever-revert would restore). **Why "Open" not "Resolved":** the SOAK forces spider ON every frame (worst case); production has spider idle ~75 % of the time per the V.7.7C.2 per-segment cooldown, so real-music p95 will land lower. But the SOAK kernel measurement also doesn't include WORLD pass + drawable presentation overhead (~0.5–1 ms). Net production p95 is *probably* below 14 ms on M2 Pro but the closure gate is the actual production capture per Matt's DM.3 procedure. **L4 (DeviceTier-aware fallback to V.7.5 2D silhouette spider on Tier 1) was explicitly NOT pulled** — the prompt requires Matt's call before introducing the Tier-1 fallback. If Matt's real-music capture shows post-L1+L2+L3 p95 still > 14 ms, L4 is the next escalation. **Tests + verification.** 45 targeted Arachne tests / 9 suites green at every lever step (`ArachneSpiderRender`, `ArachneState`, `ArachneStateBuild`, `ArachneListeningPose`, `ArachneBranchAnchors`, `PresetAcceptance`, `PresetRegression`, `PresetLoaderCompileFailure`, `StagedComposition`). `ArachneSpiderRender` golden hash unchanged at `0x000080C004000000` — spider silhouette dHash within 8-bit hamming tolerance after L1. `PresetRegression` Arachne hashes unchanged (the regression render path leaves `worldTex` unbound and slot-6/7 zeroed, so the lever changes don't surface here; real visual divergence is observed in `PresetVisualReviewTests` — RENDER_VISUAL=1 contact sheets generated at every step show no obvious silhouette/drop degradation at the harness scale). PresetAcceptance D-037 invariants pass (non-black, no white clip, beat response bounded, form complexity ≥ 2). Engine 1220 tests / 150 suites with three documented pre-existing failures unrelated to BUG-011: `MatIDDispatch.matID==1 emission path` (LM.3.2 round-4 documentation drift — test expects pre-LM.3.2 `kLumenEmissionGain = 4.0`; spawned as a separate task during this session), `SoakTestHarness.cancel` and `MetadataPreFetcher.fetch_networkTimeout` (documented parallel-load timing flakes, present pre-BUG-011 per CLAUDE.md "Test suite baseline"). App build clean. SwiftLint 0 violations on touched files (Arachne.metal not lintable; SoakTestHarnessTests.swift clean). **Carry-forward:** (a) Matt's M2 Pro real-music perf capture per the DM.3 procedure — the BUG-011 closure gate; if Arachne window p95 ≤ 14 ms / drops ≤ 8 % on a 60 s representative window, flip Status to Resolved with the measured-after numbers. (b) M3+ measurement to confirm budget holds at full feature set on actual Tier 2 silicon (M2 Pro is borderline; the architecture contract specifies M3+). (c) L4 escalation only if M2 Pro real-music p95 still > 14 ms post-tuning — would need a new D-XXX entry in [docs/DECISIONS.md](docs/DECISIONS.md) ("Arachne is M3+-only with V.7.5 2D silhouette spider fallback on Tier 1") before implementation. (d) V.7.10 cert review remains gated on this — cert sign-off can't proceed on a preset over budget on its target hardware tier. (e) MatIDDispatch test fix (pre-existing LM.3.2 documentation drift, spawned as separate task). The 16 ms SOAK gate is the in-tree regression discriminator going forward — if any of the three lever values is reverted, kernel p95 will jump back into the 22–26 ms range and the gate fires.

- **Increment LM.4.4 ⏳ 2026-05-11 — Lumen Mosaic pattern engine retired.** Third M7 review on session `2026-05-11T17-02-17Z` (same 4-track playlist re-run on the LM.4.3 build) confirmed the LM.4.3 beat-sync foundation works ("solid for Love Rehab and There There ... Pyramid Song sync is fantastic — beat lands on every piano chord") AND flagged the ripple/sweep accent layer as ineffective: *"The ripple sweep is not really doing much — it's barely noticeable. What value is it really adding?"* Honest answer: at execution-time-feasible boost levels the wavefront was invisible against the simultaneous bar pulse (both events fire on the downbeat; the panel-wide pulse dominates the local +20% Gaussian band by sheer area). Pushing the wavefront brighter would have re-introduced the LM.4.1-resolved bleach-out. The CLAUDE.md Audio Data Hierarchy rule frames the deeper issue ("beat onset events are ACCENT ONLY — NEVER PRIMARY"); the LM.4 pattern engine had become structurally redundant with the bar pulse, both occupying the same downbeat moment. **LM.4.4 deletes the pattern engine entirely.** **Files deleted:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift), [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift). **Files modified:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift) — `activePatterns` array, `barRotationCounter`, `prevBarPhase01`, `updatePatterns`, `spawnPattern`, `spawnBarRotationPattern`, `writePatternsToState`, `radialRippleOriginFromBar`, `sweepEntryFromBar`, `chooseBarPatternKind`, `lmHashU32`, `trackSeedHash32` all deleted. `updateBandCounters` simplified to beat-wrap-only (no bar wrap handling — barCounter no longer advances; consumer gone). `advancePatternEngine` simplified to just call `updateBandCounters`. `resetBeatTrackingState` no longer clears pattern pool state (it's defensively zeroed instead so any future ABI consumer reads a clean snapshot). Class shrank enough to remove the LM.4-era `swiftlint:disable type_body_length`. [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal) — `lm_pattern_radial_ripple`, `lm_pattern_sweep`, `lm_evaluate_active_patterns` evaluator functions deleted. `kPatternBoost`, `kPatternMaxSum`, `kRippleMaxRadius`, `kRippleSigmaBase`, `kSweepSigma` constants deleted. The integration site in `sceneMaterial` (`cell_intensity += pattern_contribution * kPatternBoost`) deleted. [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternEngineTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternEngineTests.swift) — Suite 9 renamed `LumenLM43CounterTests` → `LumenLM44CounterTests`; `test_barPhase01Wrap_incrementsBarCounter` + `test_noGridSignal_noBarCounterAdvance` retired and replaced with `test_barCounter_neverAdvances_afterLM44` which regression-locks the dead-counter contract; `driveBarWrap` helper deleted from the suite. **What's preserved:** the LM.3.2 cell-color dance (now driven by LM.4.3 grid-wrap counters) + the bar pulse (`kBarPulseMagnitude = 0.20`) are the entire visual story now. The `LumenPattern` / `LumenPatternKind` / `LumenLightAgent` structs and the `state.patterns[4]` tuple stay in `LumenPatternState` for GPU ABI continuity — the slot-8 buffer's byte layout is unchanged so future LM.5+ work (continuous pattern fields like breathing / noiseDrift, NOT transient bursts) could rebind to the same slots without a struct-version bump. **Verification:** 1217 engine tests (was 1237 at LM.4.3 — net −20 from deleting 19 LumenPatterns tests + 1 LM.4.3 Suite 9 test consolidation); same 3 documented pre-existing failures unchanged (MatIDDispatch matID==1 LM.3.2 calibration drift; SoakTestHarness cancel + MetadataPreFetcher networkTimeout parallel-load timing flakes). App build clean. SwiftLint touched files clean; project baseline `+1` violation in `DriftMotesGeometry.swift` (pre-existing, from a separate DM.3.3.1 commit, not introduced by LM.4.4). Lumen Mosaic golden hash unchanged (regression render path leaves slot-8 zero placeholder; with no pattern contribution path the hash is identical to LM.4.3). **Carry-forward:** LM.4.5 (full-spectrum per-track palette redesign) is the next planned increment. With the pattern engine gone, the palette redesign focuses cleanly on what actually matters: colour variety across the spectrum. Status: ⏳ awaiting Matt re-review.

- **Increment LM.4.3 ⏳ 2026-05-11 — Lumen Mosaic BeatGrid-driven triggers + ripples-as-accent.** Second M7 review on session `2026-05-11T15-56-41Z` (same 4-track playlist re-run on the LM.4.1 build) made the LM.4 / LM.3.2 trigger-source failure conclusive. Diagnostic: all four tracks fired ripples at ~2.41/sec regardless of tempo (Love Rehab 118 BPM ≈ 1.97 kicks/sec, Pyramid Song 70 BPM ≈ 1.17 kicks/sec — both produced 2.42 `beatBass` rising edges/sec). The "trigger" signal was `f.beatBass`, an FFT bass-band onset detector that fires on ~any sub-bass transient (kicks, bass-line notes, low harmonics, room rumble) — completely decoupled from the song's actual beat. Same root cause affected the LM.3.2 cell-dance band counters: cells were stepping ~2.4× faster than the song's beat, hence Matt's "color does not really follow the music in any clear way" feedback. Matt's reframing also called out the deeper architecture mistake: per-kick ripples treat onset events as primary motion, which inverts the CLAUDE.md Audio Data Hierarchy rule ("ACCENT ONLY — NEVER PRIMARY"). **LM.4.3 redesign (one commit):** (a) replace the FFT trigger with `f.beatPhase01` wrap (each grid beat) and `f.barPhase01` wrap (each grid downbeat) — accurate tempo via the DSP.2 S7 `LiveBeatDriftTracker`; (b) demote ripples to "once per measure" — remove the per-kick onset-ripple spawn path entirely; the only pattern trigger now is `barFired` (bar-counter rising edge), firing one ripple-or-sweep (mood-weighted) per musical bar; (c) cell-dance band counters now subdivide the grid: `bassCounter` ticks every beat (fastest), `midCounter` every 2 beats, `trebleCounter` every 4 beats — the LM.3.2 "team" labels are reinterpreted as rate buckets, not FFT bands. Cell-team percentages (30/35/25/10) preserved shader-side. **Files modified:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift) — new private state (`prevBeatPhase01 / prevBarPhase01` wrap-edge detection + `gridBeatsSinceMidStep / gridBeatsSinceTrebleStep` subdivision counters); `updateBandCounters(features:)` rewritten to detect grid wraps and advance counters uniformly (+1.0 each, no `beatStrength` scaling); `updatePatterns(dt:barFired:)` simplified — no more `bassFired` path; `advancePatternEngine` captures only `prevBarCounter`; `radialRippleOriginFromOnset()` deleted; `drumOnsetCounter` deleted; `resetBeatTrackingState()` updated to clear LM.4.3 wrap state. [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift) — `radialRippleDuration` restored 0.3 → 0.6 s (LM.4.1 halved it for the per-kick world; LM.4.3 per-bar spawning gives the longer lifetime plenty of headroom — ~1.4 s rest between accents on typical 4/4 at 120 BPM). [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift) — `fv()` helper signature `beatBass:` → `beatPhase01:`; new `spawnOnePatternViaBarWrap` helper; test_bassRisingEdge_spawnsRipple → test_barWrap_spawnsBarRotationPattern + new test_beatPhase01Wrap_doesNotSpawnPattern; lifecycle/expansion/sweep tests rewired through bar wraps. [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternEngineTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternEngineTests.swift) — Suite 9 fully rewritten: `test_beatPhase01Wrap_incrementsBassCounterByOne`, `test_beatPhase01HeldHigh_doesNotIncrement`, `test_midAndTrebleTickAtSubdividedRates`, `test_barPhase01Wrap_incrementsBarCounter`, `test_noGridSignal_noBarCounterAdvance`, `test_fftBeatBass_aloneDoesNotAdvanceAnyCounter`, `test_reset_zerosBandCounters`, `test_setTrackSeed_zerosBandCounters`. **Verification:** 1237 engine tests / 19 LumenPatterns / 8 LM.4.3 Suite 9 — same three documented pre-existing failures (`MatIDDispatch` LM.3.2 calibration drift + 2 parallel-load timing flakes). SwiftLint 0 violations on touched files. App build clean. **Known limitation:** no FFT fallback — if `f.beatPhase01` never wraps (pure silence; pre-grid first ~10 s of reactive sessions), counters and patterns are static. Acceptable for prepared sessions (grid is at session start); LM.4.4 may add a fallback if reactive ad-hoc sessions surface the gap. **Carry-forward:** LM.4.5 (full-spectrum per-track palette redesign) is still the next planned increment — palette breadth + the LM.4.3 beat-sync foundation together should answer Matt's "movement of color follows the music" and "variety within a narrow scope" feedback. Status: ⏳ awaiting Matt re-review on a third real-music session.

- **Increment LM.4.1 ⏳ 2026-05-11 — Lumen Mosaic ripple density + bleach-out fix.** First M7 review on session `2026-05-11T15-15-46Z` (Love Rehab → So What → There There → Pyramid Song playlist) surfaced three issues: (a) ripples fired so fast and often that individual pulses never registered — `features.csv` showed 24 `beatBass` rising edges per 10 s window at 118 BPM, i.e. 2.4 ripples/sec stacked against a 0.6 s lifetime → continuous overlap; (b) the colour palette read as nearly the same across tracks — diagnosed as additive bleach-out from cell baseline `[0.85, 1.0]` × bar pulse peak 1.30 + LM.4 pattern boost peak +0.40 = combined peak `cell_intensity` 1.70, well past the `rgba8Unorm` 1.0 albedo clamp ceiling; saturated HSV cells like `(0.10, 0.95, 0.95)` had two of three channels slammed to 1.0 on every downbeat-with-ripple frame, destroying per-cell colour identity and making mood-distinct tracks (Love Rehab `(val+0.41, arousal+0.45)` vs So What `(val−0.44, arousal+0.58)` — completely opposite valence) read as the same palette; (c) the music-sync feel weaker than LM.3.2 — same root cause as (a)+(b), the LM.4 patterns were shouting over the LM.3.2 per-cell dance instead of accenting it. **Three calibration changes (one commit):** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift) — `radialRippleDuration` 0.6 → 0.3 s (ripples now complete between kicks across the typical tempo range; at 118 BPM the gap between kicks is ~0.5 s, well above the new lifetime); [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal) — `kPatternBoost` 0.40 → 0.20 (halves pattern-driven intensity injection so cells stay below the clamp ceiling on downbeats); `kBarPulseMagnitude` 0.30 → 0.20 (LM.3.2 carry-forward — the bar pulse stacks on the pattern boost so cutting both was required; combined peak cell_intensity now ~1.20 vs 1.70). **Test updates:** [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift) — `test_fivthSpawnEvictsOldest` and `test_pool_neverExceedsPatternCount` switched from `beatBass` rising edges (80 ms-debounced) to `barPhase01` wraps (no debounce) so 5 spawns can land inside the 300 ms ripple lifetime and challenge the pool cap; without this change the new shorter lifetime would let ripples retire naturally before the pool fills and the eviction code path would never execute. **Verification:** All 18 LumenPatterns + 1191 engine tests pass except the same documented `MatIDDispatch.matID==1 emission path` pre-existing failure (LM.3.2 round-4 calibration drift). SwiftLint 0 violations on touched files; project baseline preserved. **Carry-forward / known limitation surfaced:** Matt's review also called out a deeper palette-scope limitation independent of bleach-out — the LM.3.2 palette structurally floors saturation at 0.78 and brightness at 0.80, so cells can never be dark, deep, muted, or desaturated. He wants "literally any HEX code or Pantone shade" (his words) — full color wheel, full saturation range, full brightness range, including regal purples, browns, charcoals, and dark variants of every hue. That is an LM.3.2 palette architecture redesign (track-specific custom palette cards of ~50 distinct colors drawn from the full HSV cube, with a "no pastel" guardrail: low saturation must come with low brightness so we get charcoals/browns, not pastels). Scheduled as **LM.4.5** — separate, larger increment. LM.4.1 lands the bleach + density fix independently so the underlying signal is readable while LM.4.5 is built.

- **Increment LM.4 ⏳ 2026-05-10 — Lumen Mosaic pattern engine v1 (idle / radial_ripple / sweep).** Layers transient brightness spikes on top of the LM.3.2 cell field. Drum onsets (rising-edge of `f.beatBass`, via the existing 80 ms-debounced band-counter machinery) fire a `radialRipple` from a hash-derived origin in `[0.05, 0.95]²` UV; bar-counter rising edges (LM.3.2's `barCounter`, which already handles both the `f.barPhase01` wrap path AND the every-4-bass-beats fallback for reactive mode) fire either a `radialRipple` from a separate hash family or a `sweep` from one of the four panel-edge midpoints — mood-weighted (high arousal biases 60/40 toward sweep; low arousal 60/40 toward ripple; mid-arousal 50/50). Pool capacity 4; overflowing spawns evict the oldest pattern (largest `phase`). **Patterns inject INTENSITY, not COLOUR (LM.3.2 architecture)** — each cell keeps its palette identity, the wavefront brightens whatever colour the cell already has, the frost halo at cell boundaries (round 7) also brightens through `albedo = clamp(frosted_hue × cell_intensity, …)`. **Files created:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatterns.swift) — stateless `LumenPatternFactory` enum namespace with `idle()`, `radialRipple(origin:birthTime:duration:intensity:)`, `sweep(origin:direction:birthTime:duration:intensity:)`. Defaults: `radialRippleDuration = 0.6 s`, `sweepDuration = 0.8 s`, `defaultPeakIntensity = 1.0`. Sweep direction normalised to unit length; zero-length input falls back to `(0, 1)`. Colour fields stay zero on every factory output. [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternsTests.swift) — 18 tests across 5 suites: factory value contracts (5), lifecycle (5 — spawn / phase advance / retire / reset clears / setTrackSeed clears), radial ripple expansion contract (3), sweep direction (3), pool eviction (2). **Files modified:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift) — new private LM.4 state (`activePatterns: [LumenPattern]`, `drumOnsetCounter`, `barRotationCounter`); `_tick` captures `prevBassCounter` / `prevBarCounter` before `updateBandCounters` and derives `bassFired` / `barFired` after; new `updatePatterns(dt:bassFired:barFired:)` helper handles advance → cull → spawn → snapshot; `spawnPattern(_:)` evicts the oldest by max-phase when the pool is at capacity; `spawnBarRotationPattern()` dispatches mood-weighted choice; three separate hash families avoid collision (`drumOnsetCounter ^ trackSeed` / `barRotationCounter ^ (trackSeed ^ 0xA5A5A5A5)` / `barRotationCounter ^ trackSeed`); `lmHashU32(_:)` byte-identical to the shader's `lm_hash_u32`. `resetBeatTrackingState()` extended to clear `activePatterns` + `drumOnsetCounter` + `barRotationCounter` + the zeroed `state.patterns` snapshot — the `setTrackSeed` path is load-bearing for both axes (band counters + pattern pool) so the new track paints fresh choreography from beat 1. [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal) — three new shader-side evaluators: `lm_pattern_radial_ripple(cell_uv, p)` (Gaussian band centred on `radius = phase × kRippleMaxRadius (√2)`, σ narrows from `kRippleSigmaBase (0.10)` × `(1 − 0.7 × phase)` so the wavefront sharpens as it expands); `lm_pattern_sweep(cell_uv, p)` (Gaussian band whose centre's projection onto `p.direction` is `sweep_position = phase × 2 − 1`, fixed σ `kSweepSigma (0.10)`); `lm_evaluate_active_patterns(cell_uv, lumen)` (sums up to `lumen.activePatternCount` per-pattern intensities, dispatched on `kindRaw`, clamps to `kPatternMaxSum (1.0)`). Integration in `sceneMaterial` runs after `lm_cell_intensity` — fragment uv remapped from `panel_uv ∈ [-1, +1]` into `[0, 1]²` (`cell_center_uv = panel_uv × 0.5 + 0.5`), then `cell_intensity += lm_evaluate_active_patterns(...) × kPatternBoost (0.4)`. **Address-space note (Failed Approach #44 caught):** per-pattern helpers take `LumenPattern` by value (not `constant LumenPattern&`) so the evaluator loop can copy a slot out of `lumen.patterns[]` (constant address space) into a thread-space local without the mismatch that would otherwise drop the shader silently from the loader; `PresetLoaderCompileFailureTest` caught this at the 15 vs 16 expected production preset count. **Verification:** All 18 new LumenPatterns tests pass. PresetAcceptance + PresetRegression + PresetLoaderCompileFailure + LumenPatternEngine + StagedComposition all green (58 tests across 17 suites in the touched subset). Engine full suite has one pre-existing failure (`MatIDDispatch.matID==1 → emission path` — test fixture has stale `kLumenEmissionGain = 4.0` from before LM.3.2 round 4 dropped it to 1.0; baseline-confirmed via `git stash` to be pre-existing, not introduced by LM.4). PresetRegression Lumen Mosaic golden hash unchanged at `0xF0F0C8CCCCC8F0F0` — the regression render path leaves slot-8 bound to the zero placeholder, so `activePatternCount = 0` and the pattern contribution path returns 0 unconditionally; real visual divergence is observed via `RENDER_VISUAL=1` `PresetVisualReviewTests` (deferred — needs in-engine spawn state to be ticked). **Carry-forward:** ⏳ awaiting Matt review on a real-session capture against the LM.3.2 contact-sheet's six-point checklist + the new LM.4 acceptance items: (a) drum onsets visibly produce ripples expanding from coherent origins — same track replays paint the same ripple choreography; (b) bar-rotation pattern character noticeably changes at bar boundaries (Spotify-prepared track); every-4-beats fallback feels coherent (reactive-mode track); (c) pattern + bar-pulse interaction reads as a coherent emphasis, not fighting (if it fights, halve `kPatternBoost`); (d) D-037 beat-response invariant holds on the harness's beat-heavy fixture (the LM.3.2 ceiling at silence-baseline × 2 + 1.0 stays under because the harness fixture has `barPhase01 = 0` and the pattern contribution at peak adds 0.4 to `cell_intensity ∈ [0.85, 1.0]` → 1.25–1.4 << 2.7 ceiling). LM.5 (clusterBurst + breathing + noiseDrift) is the next planned LM increment.

- **Increment LM.3.2 ✅ 2026-05-10 — Lumen Mosaic band-routed beat-driven dance (D.5 / D-LM-d5).** *M7 pass on real-music session `2026-05-10T15-44-27Z`. Matt 2026-05-10: "Awesome. Finally. The movement of the color in the cells is looking good. I'd consider this a 'pass.'" Eight calibration rounds (commits `76e21bf8` → `d4f66e21`, branch ahead of origin/main by 8 commits, NOT pushed): round 1 baseline → round 2 widened mood palette + cell density 30 → 15 → round 3 per-channel seed perturbation → round 4 HSV palette + emission gain 4 → 1 → round 5 frosted-glass surface character → round 6 beat envelope → round 7 frost in albedo → round 8 dropped beat envelope (cells hold previous palette state until next team beat — no dark "pulse off" gap). Final architecture: HSV-driven palette giving saturated jewel tones; per-cell + per-track hash drives team / period / palette-base / hue-shift; Voronoi `f2 - f1` distance bakes a clean white frost halo at cell boundaries directly into albedo (no normal-driven sub-pixel artifacts); cells stay lit between beats with the per-beat palette-step advance + bar-pulse downbeat flash carrying all rhythm coupling. Carry-forward: track-to-track colour variation could be wider (Matt's 2026-05-10 follow-up note) — first lever is `kSeedMagnitudeD` 0.50 → 0.65, schedule for LM.6 fidelity polish or earlier as a tuning pass. **LM.4** (pattern engine v1: idle / radial_ripple / sweep) is the next planned LM increment.* Original landing notes follow.

- **Increment LM.3.2 (initial landing) 2026-05-09 — Lumen Mosaic band-routed beat-driven dance (D.5 / D-LM-d5).** *Calibration round 3 applied 2026-05-09 same day after Matt's third M7-prep review: "the colors are still very similar. The pastel palette is fine for one session but I'd like to see more variety." The contact sheet was missing the per-track-seed dimension entirely — the 5-mood/energy fixtures all had `setTrackSeed = .zero`, so the harness never exercised the inter-track-variety mechanism. Round 3 added 4 per-track-seed fixtures at the four ±1 corners of the 4D seed cube + redesigned the seed perturbation: scalar perturbation of `a` (offset) and `d` (phase) was replaced with per-channel sum-balanced perturbation `(sA, sB, -(sA+sB)/2)` so different tracks land on different hue DOMINANCES, not just rotated phases of the same colour set. Magnitudes recalibrated 0.20/0.20/0.30/0.50 → **0.20/0.05/0.20/0.50** (kSeedMagnitudeB reduced because the previous 0.20 could pull `b` (chroma) into pastel territory at negative seedB; the small 0.05 stays inside the saturated regime). Real-music FNV-1a `title|artist` hashes distribute uniformly across the 4D cube; the four corner fixtures bracket the visual range. Per Round 1: every contact-sheet image looked the same — moods didn't visibly differ; "the camera can zoom in a little, 50 → 30 cells across". Per Round 2: cell density `kCellDensity` 30 → 15 (cells across 60 → 30), and palette endpoints widened so HV-HA and LV-LA produce genuinely different palette regions (cool→blue-dominant base, warm→red-dominant base) — `kPaletteACool/AWarm` widened from `(0.50, 0.50, 0.55) / (0.55, 0.45, 0.45)` (≤ 0.10 per-channel diff) to `(0.25, 0.50, 0.75) / (0.75, 0.50, 0.25)`; `kPaletteBVivid` 0.55 → 0.65; `kPaletteDComplementary/Analogous` 0.67 / 0.20 → 1.00 / 0.15. Re-captured 9-fixture contact sheet shows clearly distinct moods + 4 visibly different per-track variants (yellow / magenta-cyan-blue / red-magenta-yellow / green-cyan-yellow).* Second LM redesign in 24 hours after both LM.3 (continuous palette cycling on `accumulated_audio_time × kCellHueRate` — cells did not visibly cycle on Spotify-normalised audio because BUG-012 under-reads mid + treble bands → `accumulated_audio_time` advanced ~0.045 / sec instead of ~0.5 / sec) and LM.3.1 (agent-position-driven static-light field — Matt 2026-05-09: "fixed-color cells with brightness modulation; the bright pools dominated the visual story") were rejected in production. **LM.3.2** replaces both with: (1) cells advance their palette index *discretely on each FFT-band beat* (rising-edge of `f.beatBass / beatMid / beatTreble`, debounced 80 ms, scaled by `beatStrength = clamp(0.3 + 1.4 × max(f.bass, f.mid, f.treble), 0.3, 1.0)`); (2) cells assigned to one of four teams (30 % bass / 35 % mid / 25 % treble / 10 % static) by `lm_hash_u32(cell_id ^ lm_track_seed_hash(lumen)) % 100` — different tracks → different cells in the static team; (3) per-cell period ∈ {1, 2, 4, 8} (Pareto: ≈37.5 % / 25 % / 25 % / 12.5 %) determines how many team-beats between palette advances — fast cells dance every team beat, slow cells hold for many beats. Aggregate dance density target ~50–60 % of cells changing per second of energetic music. Brightness uniform with hash jitter `[0.85, 1.0]` plus bar pulse `1.0 + 0.30 × pow(saturate(f.bar_phase01), 8.0)`. Per-track palette seed magnitudes bumped (LM.3 → LM.3.2: 0.05/0.05/0.10/0.20 → 0.20/0.20/0.30/0.50). **Files modified:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/PresetLoader+Preamble.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/PresetLoader+Preamble.swift) — MSL `LumenPatternState` struct grew 360 → 376 B with four trailing `float` band counters (`bassCounter / midCounter / trebleCounter / barCounter`); [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Lumen/LumenPatternEngine.swift) — Swift struct extended to match; new private rising-edge state (`prevBeatBass / prevBeatMid / prevBeatTreble / prevBarPhase01`, debounce timestamps, `bassBeatsSinceBarFallback`); new private `updateBandCounters(features:)` helper extracted from `_tick` for SwiftLint 60-line gate; new private `resetBeatTrackingState()` helper called from both `reset()` and `setTrackSeed(_:)` (the latter is load-bearing — without it, an old track's accumulated counter values would carry over and the new track's cells would jump straight to a far-off palette index on the new track's first beat); [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Presets/Shaders/LumenMosaic.metal) — `sceneMaterial` rewritten for D.5 (~80 LOC); new `lm_hash_u32` Murmur-style mixer + `lm_track_seed_hash` helpers; new file-scope constants (`kPaletteStepSize = 0.137 ≈ 1/φ²`, `kBarPulseMagnitude = 0.30`, `kBarPulseShape = 8.0`, `kBassTeamCutoff = 30`, `kMidTeamCutoff = 65`, `kTrebleTeamCutoff = 90`, `kCellIntensityBase = 0.85`, `kCellIntensityJitter = 0.15`); retired `kCellHueRate`, `kAgentStaticIntensity`, `kCellMinIntensity`; [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Renderer/RayMarchPipeline.swift](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Renderer/RayMarchPipeline.swift) — `lumenPlaceholderBuffer` resized 360 → 376 B; [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternEngineTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Presets/LumenPatternEngineTests.swift) — stride test 360 → 376; new Suite 9 (10 tests) covering rising-edge increment / falling-edge no-increment / 80 ms debounce in/out / energy-scaled `beatStrength` / `barPhase01` wrap / every-4-bass-beats fallback / mid + treble independent / `reset()` zeroes counters / `setTrackSeed` zeroes counters; [docs/VISUAL_REFERENCES/lumen_mosaic/contact_sheets/LM.3.2/](docs/VISUAL_REFERENCES/lumen_mosaic/contact_sheets/LM.3.2/) — 5 PNG fixtures + README. **Verification:** Engine 1218/1219 pass (sole `MemoryReporter.residentBytes` documented env-dependent flake); SwiftLint 0 violations on touched files (baseline 55 preserved); App build green. PresetRegression Lumen Mosaic golden hash unchanged at `0xF0F0C8CCCCC8F0F0` for all 3 fixtures (regression render path uses zero-buffer placeholder; with all counters = 0 the LM.3.2 output collapses to the same dHash as LM.3). **Carry-forward:** ⏳ awaiting Matt M7 review on a real-music session against the LM.3.2 contact-sheet README's six-point checklist. Three pre-LM.3.2 LM increments stay `⚠ rejected` (LM.2 muted output, LM.3 no visible cycling on Spotify, LM.3.1 spotlit-blob backlight character). LM.4 (pattern bursts on top of cell field) is the next planned LM increment.

- **Increment DM.3 ✅ 2026-05-08 — Drift Motes Session 3 (event-driven audio routing).** Two event-driven audio reactivities arrive in the kernel: emission-rate scaling from `f.mid_att_rel` (lifetime divisor at respawn time) and drum dispersion shock from `stems.drums_beat` (radial outward velocity impulse gated by the BeatDetector envelope). The optional structural-flag scatter is deferred to DM.4 — `StructuralPrediction` is CPU-only (`AudioFeatures+Analyzed.swift`) and not on the GPU `FeatureVector`; landing it would require a struct extension violating the just-locked D-099 layout. **Files modified:** [PhospheneEngine/Sources/Renderer/Shaders/ParticlesDriftMotes.metal](PhospheneEngine/Sources/Renderer/Shaders/ParticlesDriftMotes.metal) — added two file-scope `constexpr constant` tuning constants (`kEmissionRateGain = 1.5f`, `kDispersionShockGain = 0.4f`); both `p.life` assignment sites in `motes_update` (the respawn branch and the safety-net `p.life <= 0.001` recovery) multiply random lifetime by `1 / (1 + kEmissionRateGain * max(0, f.mid_att_rel))` (the `max(0, ...)` clamp prevents negative `mid_att_rel` from extending lifetime — we use only the positive 'melody peaks' half of the deviation primitive); after the wind+turb integration and before the position update, a new branch fires when `smoothstep(0.30, 0.70, stems.drums_beat) > 0.0`, adding a radial outward impulse in the horizontal `(x, z)` plane with `0.2 × horizontal magnitude` +y lift — the BeatDetector envelope provides natural decay; damping (0.97/frame) settles the field between beats. Smoothstep absolute threshold on `stems.drums_beat` is D-026-allowed because D-026 targets FV raw bands, not stem onset envelopes (D-101). Header comment rewritten to describe post-DM.3 reality: kernel reads stems and FeatureVector at emission AND integration time. [PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Diagnostics/SoakTestHarnessTests.swift](PhospheneEngine/Tests/PhospheneEngineTests/Diagnostics/SoakTestHarnessTests.swift) — `shortRunDriftMotes` SOAK benchmark extended with a 2 Hz square wave on `stems.drumsBeat` (15 frames on / 15 off) so the dispersion-shock branch and its smoothstep evaluation are exercised every frame; `f.midAttRel` modulation already in place from DM.2. Total runtime 0.349 s. - **Increment DSP.3.4 ✅ 2026-05-05 — Three root causes fixed blocking PLANNED·LOCKED.** Live diagnostic from session `2026-05-05T21-13-05Z` (Love Rehab / Money / Pyramid Song ad-hoc reactive) showed: 12,509 consecutive frames in LOCKING with 0 in LOCKED; `beatPhase01` frozen at mean=0.99996; `grid_bpm=216` instead of ~125. Three independent bugs: **(1) BeatGrid finite horizon**: `BeatGrid.offsetBy` only shifted the ~10 recorded beats; past the last beat `computePhase` clamped `beatPhase01=1.0` permanently and `nearestBeat` returned nil → `consecutiveMisses` incremented every onset → `matchedOnsets` never reached `lockThreshold=4`. Fix: `offsetBy(seconds:horizon:)` now appends extrapolated beats at `period=60/bpm` up to a 300-second horizon and extrapolates downbeats at `barPeriod` beyond that — the grid is effectively infinite for any practical session. **(2) Hardcoded `sampleRate: 44100` in Beat This! call**: `runLiveBeatAnalysisIfNeeded` passed `sampleRate: 44100` to `analyzeBeatGrid` regardless of actual tap rate (48000 Hz). The mel spectrogram covered the wrong time range and BPM resolved as ~216 Hz instead of ~125. Fix: `VisualizerEngine.tapSampleRate: Double` stored from the `rate` parameter in the audio callback; passed to `analyzeBeatGrid(samples:sampleRate:)`. **(3) `StemSampleBuffer` snapshot undersized at 48000 Hz**: `snapshotLatest(seconds:)` computed sample count using the stored 44100 Hz init rate — a 10-second request retrieved 882,000 instead of 960,000 stereo samples (9.1875 s of real audio instead of 10 s). Fix: new `snapshotLatest(seconds:sampleRate:)` overload on `StemSampleBuffering` protocol and `StemSampleBuffer` implementation; `runLiveBeatAnalysisIfNeeded` calls it with `tapSampleRate`. 14 new tests: `BeatGridUnitTests` 5 new (horizon length, IOI period accuracy, downbeat spacing, phase validity past grid end, `nearestBeat` match at 30 s) + `StemSampleBufferRateTests` 5 new (44100 default, 48000 explicit, short window, equivalence at 44100, insufficient-data safety). **1028 engine tests; 0 SwiftLint violations; commit `7033ad09`.**

- **Increment DSP.3.5 ✅ 2026-05-05 — Halving octave correction + retry for live Beat This!** Session diagnostic `2026-05-05T22-57-57Z` revealed: Love Rehab reached PLANNED·LOCKED but at 244.770 BPM (2× true 125 BPM — double-time artefact from 10-second analysis window); Money stayed REACTIVE throughout (Beat This! returned empty grid on the short window, no retry path). **(1) `BeatGrid.halvingOctaveCorrected()`**: new public method in `Sources/DSP/BeatGrid.swift`. Halving-only — while `bpm > 160`, halve BPM and take every other beat. BPM < 80 intentionally unchanged (Pyramid Song genuinely runs at ~68 BPM; doubling would be wrong). Downbeats re-snapped to surviving beats within ±40 ms (one per beat slot); `beatsPerBar` recomputed from corrected downbeat IOI median. Applied before `offsetBy()` in the live trigger path so the extrapolated horizon also runs at the corrected BPM. **(2) Retry gate**: `liveBeatAnalysisDone: Bool` → `liveBeatAnalysisAttempts: Int`; constant `liveBeatMaxAttempts = 2`; first trigger at `liveBeatMinSeconds = 10.0 s`; retry at `liveBeatRetrySeconds = 20.0 s` when first attempt returns empty grid. Counter reset to 0 in `resetStemPipeline(for:)` on track change; capped at `liveBeatMaxAttempts` when a Spotify-prepared grid is already installed. **(3) Extraction**: `stemQueue.async` body moved to `performLiveBeatInference(mono:sampleRate:bufferStartTime:attemptNum:)` to keep `runLiveBeatAnalysisIfNeeded` within the 60-line SwiftLint gate. 4 new `BeatGridUnitTests` (double-time halved, Pyramid Song ~68 BPM no-op, 120 BPM no-op, 322 BPM halved twice). **1032 engine tests; 0 SwiftLint violations; commit `eac2e140`.**

- **Increment DSP.3.6 ✅ 2026-05-05 — Prepared BeatGrid wiring validation + install source logging.** `PreparedBeatGridWiringTests.swift` (5 tests in `Integration/`) proves the production wiring path: `StemCache.store → loadForPlayback → mirPipeline.setBeatGrid → liveDriftTracker.hasGrid`. Tests mirror the two critical lines of `resetStemPipeline(for:)` exactly (VisualizerEngine cannot be instantiated in SPM tests — requires Metal + AudioBuffer + RenderPipeline). Invariants proven: (1) non-empty cached BeatGrid → `hasGrid == true`, BPM matches, lockState ≠ .unlocked; (2) `hasGrid == true` → live inference guard is false → prepared grid protected; (3) no cache entry → `hasGrid == false` → live inference allowed; (4) `.empty` cached grid → `hasGrid == false` → live fallback still permitted; (5) track change to uncached track → grid cleared → live inference allowed again. Source-tagged `BEAT_GRID_INSTALL` logging added to three sites in `VisualizerEngine+Stems.swift`: (a) `runLiveBeatAnalysisIfNeeded` guard now logs `"LiveBeat: prepared grid present (X BPM) — skipping live inference"` and caps the counter; (b) `performLiveBeatInference` install block logs `source=liveAnalysis` with bpm/beats/meter/firstBeat and calls `sessionRecorder?.log()`; (c) `resetStemPipeline(for:)` cache-hit branch logs `source=preparedCache` (with non-empty grid details) or `source=preparedCache — empty grid` (live fallback allowed), and cache-miss branch logs `source=none`. Session.log receives one-time per-track `BeatGrid installed:` entries. Policy documented: prepared-cache grid wins unconditionally; live inference may only add a grid when none is present — it never replaces a valid prepared grid. `docs/diagnostics/DSP.3.6-prepared-beatgrid-wiring-validation.md` (6 sections: test invariants table, prepared-vs-live policy table, Money 7/4 analysis, logging formats, remaining gaps). **1037 engine tests; 0 SwiftLint violations.**

- **Increment V.7.7C: Arachne refractive dewdrops (§5.8 Snell's-law) ✅ 2026-05-07** — One shader-only commit per the prompt's atomicity guidance. **Shader (`Arachne.metal`):** Both COMPOSITE drop blocks — anchor-web (~line 742) and pool-web (~line 832) — replaced with the §5.8 Snell's-law refractive recipe sampling `worldTex` at `[[texture(13)]]`. Per-pixel: spherical-cap normal `sphN = normalize(float3(d2/rDrop, sqrt(1 − rNorm²)))` → `refract(-kViewRay, sphN, 0.752)` (air n=1.0 → water n=1.33) → sample WORLD at `uv + refr.xy × (rDrop × 2.5)` (foreground tuning per §5.8; the dead-reference `drawBackgroundWeb()` keeps `8.0 × rDrop` for §5.12 background webs) → Schlick fresnel rim `pow(1 − sphN.z, 5.0)` mixed with `kLightCol × 0.85` warm tint at `× 0.40` strength → pinpoint warm specular at the half-vector cap position with `1 − smoothstep(0, 0.20, specD)` mask → dark edge ring `smoothstep(0.85, 0.95) × (1 − smoothstep(0.95, 1.0))` × 0.5 → multiplied by the V.7.5 `(baseEmissionGain + beatAccent)` audio gain so drops still swell with the music (D-026 deviation-form preserved, ratio 2.57× ≥ 2× rule). Pool block additionally multiplies coverage by `w.opacity` (preserves V.7.5 fade semantics). `mat_frosted_glass`, the warm-amber emissive base, the cool-white pinpoint, and `glintAdd` are all deleted from both call sites — superseded. Net Arachne.metal LOC change ≈ ±0. **Half-vector type correction:** prompt's recipe declared `float3 halfVec = normalize(kL.xy + kViewRay.xy)` but the right-hand side is `float2`; Metal rejects the assignment with `cannot initialize a variable of type 'float3' with an rvalue of type 'metal::float2'`. Fixed in-flight to `float2 halfDir = normalize(kL.xy + kViewRay.xy)`; `specPos = halfDir * rDrop * 0.6` works identically (downstream code only consumed `halfVec.xy`). With `kViewRay = (0, 0, 1)` the math reduces to `normalize(kL.xy)` — the screen-space direction of the key light, exactly as §5.8 describes. The `PresetLoaderCompileFailureTest` (QR.3) caught the silent shader-compile drop — Failed Approach #44 gate working as intended. **Golden hashes:** Arachne dHash UNCHANGED at the V.7.7B values (`0xC6168E8F87868C80` across all three fixtures) — the regression render path leaves `worldTex` unbound, refraction reads zero, and the rim+specular+ring contributions sum below the dHash 9×8 luma quantization threshold. Spider forced regenerated `0x461E3E1F07870C00` → `0x461E2E1F07830C00` (3 bits drift, well under hamming ≤ 8). **Verification:** 23 targeted tests / 5 suites green; `RENDER_VISUAL=1` per-stage harness emits Arachne PNGs across silence / mid / beat fixtures (composite size grew 1.16 MB → 1.2 MB on the new drop signature); 0 SwiftLint violations on touched files. Full engine + app suites pass except the documented pre-existing flakes (`MemoryReporter.residentBytes` env-dependent, `MetadataPreFetcher.fetch_networkTimeout` parallel-load timing, `NetworkRecoveryCoordinator` debounce timing under @MainActor parallel load — all unrelated to shader-only changes). **Carry-forward:** V.7.7C.2 / V.7.8 (single-foreground build state machine: frame → radials → INWARD spiral over 60s, per-chord drop accretion, anchor blobs, completion event), V.7.7D (spider deepening + whole-scene 12 Hz vibration), V.7.10 (Matt M7 cert review). V.7.7C is **not** a cert run. D-093.

- **DSP.2 S9 ✅ 2026-05-05 — barPhase01/beatsPerBar propagated end-to-end; live Beat This! for reactive sessions.** `FeatureVector` floats 37–38 promoted from padding to `barPhase01` (0→1 phrase-level ramp, 0 in reactive mode) and `beatsPerBar` (time-signature numerator, default 4); Metal preamble struct updated; `init()` seeds `barPhase01=0 / beatsPerBar=4`. `MIRPipeline.buildFeatureVector` writes drift-tracker values on the grid path and 0/4 on the reactive path. `BeatGrid.offsetBy(_ seconds:)` added to shift buffer-relative grids to track-relative coordinates. `SpectralHistoryBuffer` ring 4 repurposed from `vocals_pitch_norm` to `bar_phase01`; dead `normalizePitch` + three pitch constants removed. `SpectralCartograph`: BR panel third row plots `bar_phase01`, label updated to "BAR φ". `VisualizerEngine+Stems.runLiveBeatAnalysisIfNeeded()`: fires once per track after 10 s of tap audio when `liveDriftTracker.hasGrid == false`; lazy-loads `DefaultBeatGridAnalyzer` on `stemQueue`; offsets grid via `offsetBy(elapsedSeconds − 10)`; installs via `mirPipeline.setBeatGrid()` on `@MainActor`. Effect: ad-hoc / reactive sessions receive phrase-level beat tracking after ≈ 10 s of listening, without any Spotify pre-analysis. **987 engine tests; 0 new SwiftLint violations; golden hashes unchanged.** Commit `b6a6095f`.

- **DSP.2 hardening ✅ 2026-05-05 — S7+S8 regression-locked; four bugs individually gated.** Tightened end-to-end thresholds (`test_loveRehab_endToEnd_producesBeats`: maxProb > 0.99, aboveHalf ≥ 100 — reflecting known-correct post-S8 values). New `BeatThisLayerMatchTests.swift`: loads `docs/diagnostics/DSP.2-S8-python-activations.json` and asserts Swift `predictDiagnostic` min/max/mean match Python reference stats within two-tier tolerances (preTfmTol=2e-3 for stem.bn1d + frontend.linear; postTfmTol=1e-2 for transformer.norm + head.linear + output stages — the looser tier covers ~0.3–0.9% delta from non-causal self-attention propagating 3 padded frames to all signal frames via softmax). Transformer blocks 0–5 excluded: Python hooks `transformer.N.ffn` (sub-block output before residual), Swift captures full-block output (after both residuals) — incompatible capture points; the output stages (beat_logits, beat_sigmoid) provide end-to-end transformer coverage. New `BeatThisBugRegressionTests.swift`: `test_frontendBlockNorms_matchOutputDim` (Bug 1 — asserts `weights.frontendBlocks[idx].norm.scale.count == expectedOutDim`); `test_bn1dAwarePadding_paddedFramesAreNearZeroPostBN` (Bug 3 — feeds 1497-frame zero spectrogram, checks `|stem.bn1d[t,mel]| < 1e-3` for padded frames t∈[1497, 1500)). Bugs 2+4 covered by layer-match test (wrong reshape scrambles stem.bn1d by >50%; wrong RoPE pairing diverges transformer output by >30%). `LiveBeatDriftTrackerTests.swift` extended: 7 new tests (MARK 9–15) covering `currentBPM` (no-grid zero + grid BPM match), `currentLockState` (no-grid unlocked), `relativeBeatTimes` (no-grid empty; count ceiling; past beats negative; upcoming beats positive). **975 engine tests / 103 suites; 0 SwiftLint violations.**

- **DSP.2 S8 ✅ 2026-05-05 — BeatThisModel fixed; S7's drift tracker live in production.** Four bugs found and fixed via the layer-diff harness shipped between commits `49315657..b9687cbc`: (1) frontend block had `partial → norm(wrong inDim shape) → conv → GELU` instead of PyTorch's `partial → conv → norm(out_dim) → GELU`; (2) stem reshape `[T,F] → [1,F,T,1]` was a byte-reinterpretation, not a transpose, scrambling the mel spectrogram into the conv; (3) BatchNorm1d transformed zero-padded spectrogram into non-zero `shift` values that bled through the stem conv at the time-axis right edge — fixed by pre-padding with `-shift/scale` per mel so the padded region maps to zero post-BN, matching PyTorch's zero-padding semantics; (4) RoPE pairing — Swift `applyRoPE4D` and `applyRoPE` (transformer) used half-and-half pairing `(x[i], x[D/2+i])` but `rotary_embedding_torch.rotate_half` pairs adjacent elements `(x[2i], x[2i+1])`, completely wrong attention dot products. Fix: reshape last dim D → (D/2, 2), slice the inner-2 axis for each pair, compute the standard 2D rotation, stack back. Result: love_rehab.m4a output max sigmoid 0.9999 vs reference 0.9999, 126 frames > 0.5 vs reference 124, 59 beats detected vs 59 in ground-truth fixture. `BeatThisActivationDumper` CLI executable + `Scripts/dump_beatthis_activations.py` (with sub-module hooks inside the partial-FT block) shipped as the lasting layer-diff harness — used to find every one of the four bugs and locked into the repo so future regressions are catchable. `test_loveRehab_endToEnd_producesBeats` now passes outright (no `withKnownIssue` wrapper) — the canonical "S7 is engaged in production" milestone.

- **Increment DSP.2 Session 7: LiveBeatDriftTracker + MIRPipeline integration — 2026-05-04** — `LiveBeatDriftTracker.swift` in `Sources/DSP/`: `@unchecked Sendable` final class, NSLock-guarded. Per-onset EMA drift tracker (α=0.4 per matched onset) against an offline `BeatGrid`. Search window ±50 ms; tight-match ±30 ms gates the lock counter (`unlocked → locking → locked` after 4 tight matches). `nearestBeat(to:within:)` bisect-search; phase computed as `(playbackTime + drift − beats[idx]) / period` clamped [0, 1]. `barPhase01 = (beatsSinceDownbeat + beatPhase01) / beatsPerBar`. No-onset decay τ=1 s after 2× medianBeatPeriod silence. `BeatGrid` extended with three lookup helpers (`beatIndex(at:)` bisect, `localTiming(at:)` returning `(period, beatsSinceDownbeat)`, `medianBeatPeriod`) plus internal `nearestBeat(to:within:)`. `MIRPipeline` gains `liveDriftTracker: LiveBeatDriftTracker` (always present), `setBeatGrid(_:)` setter, and a fork in `buildFeatureVector`: when the tracker has a grid the cached path drives `beatPhase01`/`beatsUntilNext` (using `self.elapsedSeconds` as the playback clock — already track-relative via `mir.reset()` in `VisualizerEngine+Capture.swift:127`); otherwise the legacy `BeatPredictor` path runs. `BeatPredictor` doc-deprecated as reactive-mode-only fallback (no `@available(*, deprecated)` annotation — would cascade warnings into the warnings-as-errors xcconfig app build). `VisualizerEngine+Stems.resetStemPipeline(for:)` now calls `mirPipeline.setBeatGrid(cached.beatGrid)` on cache hit, `setBeatGrid(nil)` otherwise. Tests: 8 `LiveBeatDriftTrackerTests` + 4 `BeatGridUnitTests` + 3 `MIRPipelineDriftIntegrationTests` = 15 new. App-layer wiring test deferred — change is two lines mirroring the existing `setStemFeatures` pattern; engine integration tests cover behavior. `PresetVisualReviewTests` arguments extended to `["Arachne", "Gossamer", "Volumetric Lithograph"]`. **Golden hashes unchanged**: regression tests use prebuilt `FeatureVector` fixtures with `beatPhase01=0` (default) — they bypass `MIRPipeline` entirely. Quality reel re-record + Pyramid Song / Money / so_what subjective sign-off pending.

- **Increment DSP.2 Session 5: BeatGridResolver + BeatGrid — 2026-05-04** — `BeatGrid.swift` (Sendable, Hashable, Codable value type in `Sources/DSP/`) + `BeatGridResolver.swift` in `Sources/DSP/`. Algorithm matches Beat This! minimal postprocessor: 7-frame max-pool → keep local maxima above 0.5 threshold → ±1-frame adjacent-peak dedup → snap downbeat candidates to nearest beat within ±2 frames (40 ms) → BPM via trimmed-mean IOI (D-075 method, no octave clamp) → `beatsPerBar = round(median_downbeat_IOI / beat_period)` (Python reference `beats_per_bar_from_downbeats`). `BeatGrid` placed in `Sources/DSP/` (not `Session/`) to avoid circular import: `Session → DSP`, not vice versa. 8 unit tests (`BeatGridResolverUnitTests`: emptyInput, belowThreshold, singlePeak, maxPool dedup, BPM=120, beatsPerBar 4/4, beatsPerBar 3/4, downbeatSnap discard) + 24 golden fixture tests (`BeatGridResolverGoldenTests`: 6 fixtures × 4 assertions — beats ≥95% within ±20ms, downbeats ≥90% within ±40ms, BPM within ±0.5, meter correct). Pyramid Song meter=3 (load-bearing irregular-meter gate) passes. **945 engine tests / 102 suites; 0 SwiftLint violations.**

- **Increment DSP.2 Session 4: BeatThisModel real weights + PartialFTTransformer frontend — 2026-05-04** — `BeatThisModel+Weights.swift` + `BeatThisModel+Frontend.swift` + `BeatThisModel+Graph.swift` updated in `Sources/ML/`. Full weight loading from 161 `.bin` tensors; BN fusion at load time (`fuseBeatThisBN` via vDSP). `BeatThisModel+Frontend.swift`: PartialFTTransformer — BN1d → Conv2d(4×3) stem, 3× PartialFTTransformerBlock (F-direction + T-direction batched attention/FFN + BN2d + Conv2d(2×3) downsampling), rearrange "b c f t → b t (c f)" + Linear(1024→128) projection. - **Increment DSP.2 Session 3: BeatThisModel MPSGraph encoder — 2026-05-04** — `BeatThisModel.swift` + `BeatThisModel+Graph.swift` + `BeatThisModel+Ops.swift` in `Sources/ML/`. Complete Beat This! small0 transformer encoder as a fixed MPSGraph with zero-weight init (S4 replaces with checkpoint). Architecture: input projection (128→128), 6 transformer blocks (RMSNorm pre-norm + multi-head attention with per-head gating + FFN GELU), post-norm, SumHead (additive: beats=col0+col1, downbeats=col1). Three macOS-14 workarounds: RMSNorm manual (`reductionSum(x²)/D + ε → squareRoot → divide → multiply γ`); SDPA manual `Q@Kᵀ/√D → softmax → @V`; RoPE precomputed `[1, tMax, headDim/2]` cos/sin constant tables. Fixed-T_max=1500 graph pads input, runs full forward pass, slices output to `frameCount`. Pre-allocated UMA `inputBuffer` reused across calls (zero-copy path). `BeatLinearSpec` struct keeps `buildLinear` at 4 params (SwiftLint gate). `CorePrediction` internal struct replaces 3-tuple (large_tuple gate). 5 new tests (graphBuilds + inputProjectionShape + outputShape_T10 + outputShape_T1497 + outputRangeIsFinite). **929 engine tests / 100 suites; 0 SwiftLint violations.** Commit `c71569b1`.

- **Increment DSP.2 Session 1: Beat This! architecture audit + weight vendoring — 2026-05-04** — Repo cloned at commit `9d787b9797eaa325856a20897187734175467074`, MIT confirmed. `small0` chosen: 2,101,352 params, 8.4 MB FP32. 161 tensors vendored under `PhospheneEngine/Sources/ML/Weights/beat_this/` (Git LFS). MIT attribution. **Key findings for S2/S3:** (a) preprocessing confirmed: n_fft=1024, hop=441, sr=22050, n_mels=128, f_min=30, f_max=11000, mel_scale="slaney" area-norm, power=1, log=`log1p(1000×mel)`; (b) SumHead is additive: `beat_logits = beat_linear_out + downbeat_linear_out` (beats are a superset of downbeats, not a softmax over classes); (c) three MPSGraph workarounds required in S3: RMSNorm manual, SDPA manual matmul+softmax (macOS 14 target), RoPE manual cos/sin; (d) single `RotaryEmbedding(head_dim=32)` shared across all 9 blocks — precompute once; (e) CPU inference timing ~415–530 ms, MPS expected ~100–150 ms but must be measured in S4; (f) `torchaudio` cannot load .m4a without `torchcodec` — use ffmpeg subprocess. 919 engine tests; 0 SwiftLint violations. Commits `afb75954..9cd0efb8`.

Periodic Hann window (N=1024); reflect center-padding; `vDSP_fft_zrip` STFT (scale = 1/(2×sqrt(N)) = 1/64); Slaney mel filterbank with **continuous Hz interpolation** (critical: integer bin-index approach underestimates by ~12%); `vvlog1pf(1000×mel)`. - **Increment V.7.7: Arachne WORLD pillar + background dewy webs ✅ 2026-05-05** — *Status correction (2026-05-07): see V.7.7A; full WORLD pillar deferred to V.7.7B. - **Arachne architecture pivot: compositing layers, not constant tweaking (D-072) — 2026-05-02** — V.7.5 M7 review found that the V.5 build still reads as a stylized 2D bullseye despite every spec'd change landing mechanically. - **U.11 follow-up: Spotify `/items` schema fix + pre-fetched track threading + `preview_url` capture (D-070)** — Three cascading bugs diagnosed via live testing and Spotify Web API documentation review. (1) `/items` response uses `"item"` key for the track object; `"track"` is deprecated — `item["track"]` returned nil for every item, producing an empty list. (2) `SessionManager`'s own `PlaylistConnector` (client-credentials) was re-fetching after OAuth connector succeeded → 401 → reactive fallback. Fixed by adding `startSession(preFetchedTracks:source:)` and threading `[TrackIdentity]` through the full callback chain; `IdleView` routes by source type (not `tracks.isEmpty`) so Spotify always uses the pre-fetched path. (3) Spotify `fields` query parameter silently returned `{}` empty dicts; removed. Added `market=from_token` (prevents null tracks for region-restricted content). (4) `preview_url` is available inline in the `/items` response — captured in `TrackIdentity.spotifyPreviewURL` (hint field, excluded from `Equatable`/`Hashable`/`Codable`); `PreviewResolver` short-circuits to it, bypassing iTunes Search API for the ~95% of Spotify tracks that have a preview. Net: 19/19 tracks parsed, 17/19 prepared (2 have no preview on Spotify's side).
- **SpotifyWebAPIConnector code review cleanup** — Six issues found and fixed. (1) Dead code: `queue(accessToken:)` removed from `SpotifyWebAPIConnecting` protocol and implementation — never called, also bypassed `tokenProvider` and hardcoded `retried: true`, making 401 recovery impossible. (2) Dead helper `parseQueueData` removed. (3) `makeTracksURL(offset:)` offset parameter removed — always called with `0`; pagination follows API-provided `next` URLs. (4) Cache-check ordering in `PreviewResolver.resolvePreviewURL`: Spotify fast path unconditionally wrote to cache on every call; moved the existing-cache check above it. (5) `TrackIdentity.Codable` serialized `spotifyPreviewURL` despite it being documented as a transient hint; added explicit `CodingKeys` enum and `init(from:)` that always decodes `spotifyPreviewURL = nil`. (6) Stale `PreviewResolver` class doc updated. 5 new tests added (3 in `PreviewResolverTests`, 2 in `SpotifyWebAPIConnectorTests`). **894 engine tests (92 suites); 305 app tests; 0 SwiftLint violations.**

Final rubric: **11/15, meetsAutomatedGate=true, certified=false pending M7**. Arachne golden hash: `(steady: 0xC4808C068EDFAE00, beatHeavy: 0xC4808C068EDFAE00, quiet: 0xC4808C068EDFAE00)`. Spider forced hash: `0x44381C2707D72E00`. **889 engine tests (92 suites); 0 SwiftLint violations.** M7 outcome 2026-05-01: rendered output matches `10_anti_neon_stylized_glow.jpg` (D-071); resolution scheduled as V.7.5 + V.7.6. Arachne `certified` flag rolled back to false; v4 golden hashes preserved as the V.7.5 baseline.

- **Increment 3.5.11: Gossamer SDF correction + v3 acceptance** — Fixed inverted SDF in `gossamerSpiralDist` and `gossamerHubDist` (`abs(fract−0.5)` → `min(fract, 1−fract)`): the old formula gave 0 in thread gaps and 0.5 on threads, making the entire capture zone render as a filled disc instead of a web. Also corrected D-037 acceptance invariant 3: brightness formula changed to `0.12 + f.bass×0.76 + bassRel×0.12` so silence (f.bass=0) is dim and steady music (f.bass≈0.5) is lit; beat flash reduced 0.65→0.30. Includes v3 geometry: 17 explicit irregular spoke angles, off-center hub at (0.465, 0.32), kWebRadius 0.42→0.44, elliptical stretch removed. D-042. Corrected SDF (`min(fract, 1−fract)`) for spiral threads. Pool webs mapped to 3D at varying depths z∈[−0.4,1.4]; anchor web always at (0,0,0.2). Spider always placed on anchor web, fixing Z-depth mismatch. Miss-ray glow `exp2(−minWebDist×14)` ensures D-037 formComplexity. `directPresetFragmentBuffer2` (buffer(7)) infrastructure for spider GPU struct. D-041. 444 tests; pre-existing failures unchanged.

- **Increment 4.3: SessionPlanner** — `DefaultSessionPlanner` composing `PresetScoring` + `TransitionDeciding` into a greedy forward-walk pre-session planner. Produces `PlannedSession` — ordered list of `PlannedTrack` entries each carrying score breakdown, transition decision, and timing. `planAsync` accepts a precompile closure (injected, keeps Orchestrator free of Renderer dependency). Synchronous `plan()` is deterministic: same inputs → byte-identical output. `PlannedSession.track(at:)` / `.transition(at:tolerance:)` for O(N) playback-time lookups. `PlanningWarning` surfaces degradation events (noEligiblePresets, forcedFamilyRepeat, budgetExceeded). `SessionPlanningError` covers emptyPlaylist, emptyCatalog, precompileFailed. 13 unit tests. - **Increment 4.2: TransitionPolicy** — `DefaultTransitionPolicy` implementing `TransitionDeciding` protocol. Structural boundary trigger (confidence ≥ 0.5, 2.5 s lookahead) takes priority over duration-expired timer fallback. `TransitionDecision` value type: trigger, scheduledAt, style, duration, confidence, rationale. Style negotiated from `transitionAffordances` + energy (cut preferred at energy > 0.7, crossfade otherwise). Crossfade duration scales linearly 2.0 s→0.5 s with energy. 12 unit tests. D-033 in DECISIONS.md. 374 tests total; 4 pre-existing Apple Music env failures unchanged.
- **Increment 4.1: PresetScorer** — `DefaultPresetScorer` implementing `PresetScoring` protocol. Four weighted sub-scores: mood (0.30), stemAffinity (0.25), sectionSuitability (0.25), tempoMotion (0.20). Two multiplicative penalties: family-repeat (0.2×) and fatigue smoothstep (60/120/300s cooldown by `FatigueRisk`). Hard exclusions gate perf-budget breakers and the currently-playing preset. `PresetScoreBreakdown` exposes all sub-scores for introspection. `PresetScoringContext` is a fully Sendable value snapshot using monotonic `elapsedSessionTime` — no `Date.now()` inside the scorer (guarantees determinism). `DeviceTier` enum added to Shared. `stemAffinity: [String: String]` added to `PresetDescriptor` (was in JSON sidecars, now decoded). 13 unit tests. D-032 in DECISIONS.md. 362 tests total; 5 pre-existing failures unchanged.
- **Increment 4.0: Enriched preset metadata schema** — `PresetMetadata.swift` with `FatigueRisk`, `TransitionAffordance`, `SongSection`, `ComplexityCost`. `PresetDescriptor` extended with 7 new Orchestrator-facing fields (`visual_density`, `motion_intensity`, `color_temperature_range`, `fatigue_risk`, `transition_affordances`, `section_suitability`, `complexity_cost`), all optional in JSON with fallback-on-missing / warn-on-malformed decoding. All 11 built-in preset JSON sidecars back-filled. 6 new `PresetDescriptorMetadataTests`. D-029 in DECISIONS.md. (Pulled forward from Phase 5.1.)
- **SwiftLint L-1 structural cleanup** — Pure mechanical refactor: zero logic changes, zero new public API. Reduced from 24 → 0 violations by extracting overlong functions and splitting oversized files into extension files. New files: `StemAnalyzer+RichMetadata.swift`, `MIRPipeline+Recording.swift`, `AudioInputRouter+SignalState.swift`, `RayMarchPipeline+PipelineStates.swift`, `RenderPipeline+FeedbackDraw.swift`, `RenderPipeline+PresetSwitching.swift`, `PresetLoader+WarpPreamble.swift`, `VisualizerEngine+Capture.swift`, `VisualizerEngine+InitHelpers.swift`, `VisualizerEngine+PublicAPI.swift`. All helpers private/internal only. 349 tests pass (4 pre-existing Apple Music environment failures unchanged).
- **SwiftLint L-0 cleanup** — Auto-corrected comma/colon/operator spacing; fixed identifier names (single-letter variable renames); fixed 2 force-unwrap violations; fixed orphaned doc comment; targeted `disable/enable` around the CSV row-writing block in `SessionRecorder`; fixed multiline-arguments in `StemAnalyzer`, `InputLevelMonitor`, `VisualizerEngine+Audio`. Reduced from 166 → 24 violations (structural file/function-length refactors deferred to a dedicated increment).
- **D-030: SpectralHistoryBuffer + SpectralCartograph** — 16 KB UMA ring buffer at buffer(5) carrying 5×480 sample trails (valence, arousal, beat_phase01, bass_dev, bar_phase01 — originally vocals_pitch_norm, repurposed to bar_phase01 in DSP.2 S9). `SpectralCartograph` preset: first `instrument`-family four-panel MIR diagnostic. `PresetCategory.instrument` added. CLAUDE.md GPU Contract corrected (buffer(0)=FeatureVector, buffer(5)=SpectralHistory). 15+ new tests.
- **BeatPredictor timing fix** — `beatPhase01` was always 0 in production because `MIRPipeline.processAnalysisFrame` passes `time: 0` to every `BeatPredictor.update()` call; `lastBeatTime > 0` guard silently rejected the first onset, so `hasPeriod` never became true. Fixed by internal `elapsedTime` accumulation from `deltaTime`, independent of the `time` parameter. Guards changed from `> 0` to `>= 0`.
- **InputLevelMonitor** — continuous tap-quality assessment (peak dBFS + spectral balance → green/yellow/red grade). Peak-only classification after session 2026-04-17 revealed treble-ratio thresholds produced false positives on bass-heavy tracks. Logs quality transitions to session.log; shown in debug overlay.
- **MV-3: Beyond-Milkdrop extensions** — `StemFeatures` expanded 32→64 floats (128→256 bytes, D-028). Three sub-increments: (a) per-stem rich metadata `{onsetRate, centroid, attackRatio, energySlope}` computed in `StemAnalyzer.computeRichFeatures()` via RMS EMAs (τ=50ms/500ms), spectral centroid, leaky-integrator onset rate; (b) `BeatPredictor` class (IIR period from onset rising edges) → `FeatureVector.beatPhase01/beatsUntilNext` for anticipatory pre-beat animation; (c) `PitchTracker` (YIN via vDSP_dotpr, key fix: advance to CMNDF local minimum before parabolic interpolation) → `StemFeatures.vocalsPitchHz/Confidence`. Metal preamble and Swift structs updated byte-for-byte. `VolumetricLithograph.metal` uses `beat_phase01` for anticipatory zoom ramp (`approachFrac * 0.004`) and `vl_pitchHueShift()` for pitch→hue mapping. 9 new unit tests across `StemAnalyzerMV3Tests`, `BeatPredictorTests`, `PitchTrackerTests`. (D-028)
- **MV-1: Milkdrop-correct deviation primitives** — `FeatureVector` expanded 32→48 floats (128→192 bytes), `StemFeatures` expanded 16→32 floats (64→128 bytes). Nine new FV deviation fields (`bassRel/Dev`, `midRel/Dev`, `trebRel/Dev`, `bassAttRel`, `midAttRel`, `trebAttRel`) derived in `MIRPipeline.buildFeatureVector()` as `xRel = (x - 0.5) * 2.0`, `xDev = max(0, xRel)`. Eight new StemFeatures deviation fields (`{vocals,drums,bass,other}EnergyRel/Dev`) derived in `StemAnalyzer.analyze()` via per-stem EMA (decay 0.995). Metal preamble structs in `PresetLoader+Preamble.swift` updated to match. `VolumetricLithograph.metal` updated as reference implementation: all four FeatureVector fallback drivers converted from absolute-threshold to deviation form. `RelDevTests.swift` (4 contract tests) gates the invariants. (D-026)
- **Increment 3.5.7: Stalker preset** — Third and final preset in the Arachnid Trilogy. Bioluminescent spider silhouette traverses a dim static background web. Articulated 8-leg alternating-tetrapod gait phase-locks to BPM via soft pull (no snap). Phosphene-exclusive: sustained low-attack-ratio bass (bassAttackRatio < 0.55 held ≥ 0.75s) triggers the listening pose (front legs raised, gait frozen) while transient kick-drum bass does not — distinguishes vibration character that Milkdrop's vocabulary cannot. `StalkerGait.swift` (pure gait solver with 2-segment IK, listening blend, beat easing). `StalkerState.swift` (scene mode state machine + sustained-bass accumulator + GPU buffer flush, 352 bytes). `Stalker.metal`: 2-threadgroup dispatch (web + spider). `StalkerGPU` struct at object/mesh buffer(1). D-026/D-019 compliant. 16 unit tests (8 gait + 8 state) in `StalkerGaitTests.swift` / `StalkerStateTests.swift`. Arachnid Trilogy complete: Arachne (mesh construction), Gossamer (mv_warp silk resonance), Stalker (mesh predator). Orchestrator family-repeat penalty naturally prevents two trilogy presets appearing consecutively. 455 tests total; 4 pre-existing Apple Music environment failures unchanged.
- **Increment 3.5.6: Gossamer preset** — Bioluminescent hero-web as sonic resonator. Single SDF-drawn static web (12 radials + Archimedean capture spiral) with up to 32 vocal-pitch-keyed propagating color waves. Emission gates on `vocalsPitchConfidence > 0.35 OR |vocalsEnergyDev| > 0.05`. Wave hue baked from YIN pitch at emission, saturation from other-stem density, amplitude from vocals_energy_dev. mv_warp pass accumulates decaying echoes (decay=0.955). Ambient drift floor guarantees ≥2 waves at silence. Fragment buffer(6) binding via `pipeline.setDirectPresetFragmentBuffer` / `directPresetFragmentBuffer`. `GossamerState.swift` owns a 32-entry pool + 528-byte GossamerGPU MTLBuffer. 8 unit tests in `GossamerStateTests.swift`. 435 tests total; 4 pre-existing Apple Music environment failures unchanged.
- **Increment 3.5.5: Arachne preset** — Bioluminescent spider web mesh shader. `ArachneState.swift` manages 12-web pool with beat-measured stage lifecycle (anchorPulse→radial→spiral→stable→evicting), drum-driven spawn accumulator, LCG PRNG, `MTLBuffer` GPU flush. `Arachne.metal`: object shader dispatches 12 mesh threadgroups; 64-thread mesh shader emits hub cap + anchor dots + radial spokes + spiral segments per web; fragment applies D-019 warmup, bass quiver, MV-3b beat anticipation. Organic family (`PresetCategory.organic` added, D-038). Quiver wave phase-locked to beat_phase01; exp2(-dist*3) bioluminescent glow falloff; sat=0.92. 8 unit tests in `ArachneStateTests.swift`. `PresetCategory.allCases.count` updated to 14. 427 tests total; 4 pre-existing Apple Music environment failures unchanged.
- **Increment 5.2: Preset Acceptance Checklist** — `PresetAcceptanceTests.swift`: 4 parametrized invariant tests over all 11 production presets (44 test cases). Invariants: non-black at silence; no white clip on non-HDR paths; beat response ≤ 2× continuous + 1.0; form complexity ≥ 2. ## Linked Frameworks

Metal, MetalKit, MetalPerformanceShadersGraph, AVFoundation, Accelerate, ScreenCaptureKit (Info.plist only), MusicKit.

## Development Constraints

- **Team**: Matt (product/design direction) + Claude Code (implementation).
- **Platform**: macOS only. Mac mini primary dev/deploy target.
- **Performance target**: 60fps at 1080p on Apple Silicon.
- **Dependencies**: Minimize external. Prefer Apple frameworks.
- **Learning stays local**: On-device only. No cloud, no telemetry.
- **License**: MIT.
- **Git history is maintained on github.com/hoaxpoet/phosphene.** Each increment lands as one or more commits with the increment ID in the message (e.g., `[SB.1] Routing: convert drums to drumsEnergyDev (D-026)`). For change diagnosis, prefer `git log`, `git diff`, and `git bisect` over reconstructing from documentation. `ENGINEERING_PLAN.md` and `DECISIONS.md` remain authoritative for intent and rationale; git is authoritative for what changed.
